@196B PA'I PHYOGS TZAM ZHIG ,BSTAN PA YIN PAS BSLAB TSUL RGYAS
PAR NI, ,SNGAGS KYI LAM RIM RNAMS LAS SHES DGOS SO, ,DE LTA'I
TSUL GYIS BSLAB NA MDO SNGAGS KYI, ,GNAD DON THAMS CAD BSDUS
PA'I

LAM GYI LUS, ,YONGS SU RDZOGS LA BSLAB PAR 'GYUR BAS NA, ,DAL PA
THOB PA DON DANG LDAN PAR 'GYUR, ,KUN MKHYEN RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA
RIN PO CHE, ,RANG DANG GZHAN GYI RGYUD LA RGYAS PAR BYED, ,NUS
PA YIN

PAS LAM BZANG 'DI 'DRA LA, ,BLO DANG LDAN PA RNAMS KYIS 'BAD PAR
RIGS, ,DE LTAR GSUNG RAB KUN GYI GNAD BSDUS BA, ,SHING RTA CHEN
PO GNYIS KYI LAM GYI SROL, ,KUN MKHYEN SAR BGROD SKYE BO MCHOG
GI LUGS,

MDO SNGAGS GNYIS KA'I LAM LAG CES PA'I CHOS, ,DNGON MTHO NGES
LEGS THAMS CAD SGRUB PA'I THABS, ,BYANG CHUB LAM GYI RIM PA'I
TSIG BCAD 'DI, ,YAB RJE RGYAL BA GNYIS PA'I GDAMS PA MCHOG ,

LAM RIM CHE CHUNG GNYIS LAS BSDUS TE BKOD, ,BDAG NYID CHEN PO'I
LEGS BSHAD PHUL BYUNG MCHOG ,YOD BZHIN 'DI 'DRA YAN LAG BRGYAD
LDAN GYI, ,RGYA MTSO'I 'GRAM DU BA TSA'I KHRON PA DANG, ,MTSUNGS
PAS

RANG NYID DAL BA TZAM DU ZAD, ,BRJOD BYA SNGA MAR MA BSHAD 'DIR
BRJOD MIN, ,BRJOD BYED BSDEBS LEGS SNYAN PAS MDZES MIN KYANG,
,TSIG NYUNG DON 'DUS BSHAR SBYANG 'KHYER BDE BAR, ,KHUNGS DANG
SPREL NAS TSIGS

SU BCAD DE BSDEBS, ,THA CHAD BYIS BLOS MA RTOG LOG RTOG GI,

SNYING

NAS BSHAGS, ,'DIR 'BAD DGE BA ZLA ZER LTAR DKAR BA, ,GANG DE

LUGS KU MUD TSAL, ,BZHAD CING 'GRO BA'I TSA GDUNG SEL PHYIR
BSDO,, ,,CES BYANG CHUB

@197A *, ,LAM GYI RIM PA'I GDAMS PA'I TSIGS SU BCAD PA KUN
MKHYEN BDE LAM ZHES BYA BA 'DI NI RANG GI GAM DU NYE BAR 'KHOD
CING LUGS GNYIS LA RNAM DPYOD MI DMAN PA DKA' BCU NGAG DBANG
CHOS LDAN MING GZHAN

SHES RABS YANG YANG BSKUL ZHING, GZHAN YANG BKA' SDE SNOD LA
SBYANGS PA CHE ZHING RNAM DPYOD YANGS PA'I MTSO BDUN DGON GSAR
GYI T'A BLA MA KA BCU BKA' 'GYUR PA BLO BZANG TSUL KHRIMS, ,RANG
GI GAM DU NYE BAR 'KHOD DE LAG

G-YOG TSUL MTHUN BYED MI SDOM BRTZON CHOS LA DKAR ZHING NYAMS
LEN LA MOS PA'I DAD 'DUN CAN LHUN 'GRUB RGYA MTSO SOGS, ,DON
GNYER PA 'GA' ZHIG GIS KYANG BSKUL BA DANG, ,RANG NYID BAG CHAGS
'JOG CING SKAL MNYAM

'GA' ZHIG LA PHAN PA'ANG SRID SNYAM PA'I BSAM PAS SNYOM LAS PA
NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG CHOS LDAN DPAL BZANG PO ZHES BGYI BAS SPYOD
PA SPYI BSLAB YAN CHAD LAM RIM CHEN MO DANG, ,ZHI LHAG GNYIS LAM
RIM CHUNG BA NAS TSIG SNA

BSDUS; SHES BYED KYI LUNGS 'DREN 'OS RNAMS SKABS DANG SBYAR,
RNGOG LO CHEN PO'I THUGS SRAS DGE BSHES GRO LUNG PA BLO GROS
'BYUNG GNAS KYI BSTAN RIM, RJE NYID KYIS KYANG THUGS BRTZES CHE
BAR MDZAD PA DE LAS KYANG LUNG

'GA' ZHIG DRANGS, RANG NYID KYIS LAM RIM GYI KHRID RGYUN, PAn
CHEN CHOS KYI RGYAL PO BLO BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN DANG,
RGYAL DBANG THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG RGYA MTSO
GNYIS LAS BRGYUD PA GNYIS KA THOB PA'I

MAN NGAG GIS BRGYAN TE BSHAR SBYANG BYED PAR 'KHYER BDE BA'I
PHYIR TSIG BCAD DU BKOD PA'I YI GE PA NI BSKUL BA PO DPYOD LDAN
DKA' BCU SHES DAR BA'O, ,'DIS KYANG RGYAL BSTAN SPYI DANG KHYAD
PAR RGYAL BA

GYUR 'GRO BA THAMS CAD PHAN BDE'I DPAL BZANG PO LA SPYOD PAR
